## <span id="Roles"></span> `Roles`

Library for managing addresses assigned to a Role.

- [`add(struct Roles.Role role, address account)`][Roles-add-struct-Roles-Role-address-]
- [`remove(struct Roles.Role role, address account)`][Roles-remove-struct-Roles-Role-address-]
- [`has(struct Roles.Role role, address account)`][Roles-has-struct-Roles-Role-address-]
### <span id="Roles-add-struct-Roles-Role-address-"></span> `add(struct Roles.Role role, address account)` (internal)

give an account access to this role



### <span id="Roles-remove-struct-Roles-Role-address-"></span> `remove(struct Roles.Role role, address account)` (internal)

remove an account's access to this role



### <span id="Roles-has-struct-Roles-Role-address-"></span> `has(struct Roles.Role role, address account)  bool` (internal)

check if an account has this role

## <span id="Pausable"></span> `Pausable`

Base contract which allows children to implement an emergency stop mechanism.

- [`whenNotPaused()`][Pausable-whenNotPaused--]
- [`whenPaused()`][Pausable-whenPaused--]
- [`onlyPauser()`][PauserRole-onlyPauser--]
- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(address sender)`][Pausable-initialize-address-]
- [`paused()`][Pausable-paused--]
- [`pause()`][Pausable-pause--]
- [`unpause()`][Pausable-unpause--]
- [`isPauser(address account)`][PauserRole-isPauser-address-]
- [`addPauser(address account)`][PauserRole-addPauser-address-]
- [`renouncePauser()`][PauserRole-renouncePauser--]
- [`_addPauser(address account)`][PauserRole-_addPauser-address-]
- [`_removePauser(address account)`][PauserRole-_removePauser-address-]
- [`constructor()`][Context-constructor--]
- [`_msgSender()`][Context-_msgSender--]
- [`_msgData()`][Context-_msgData--]
- [`Paused(address account)`][Pausable-Paused-address-]
- [`Unpaused(address account)`][Pausable-Unpaused-address-]
- [`PauserAdded(address account)`][PauserRole-PauserAdded-address-]
- [`PauserRemoved(address account)`][PauserRole-PauserRemoved-address-]
### <span id="Pausable-whenNotPaused--"></span> `whenNotPaused()`

Modifier to make a function callable only when the contract is not paused.

### <span id="Pausable-whenPaused--"></span> `whenPaused()`

Modifier to make a function callable only when the contract is paused.

### <span id="Pausable-initialize-address-"></span> `initialize(address sender)` (public)





### <span id="Pausable-paused--"></span> `paused()  bool` (public)




#### *Returns*
- **true**: if the contract is paused, false otherwise.

### <span id="Pausable-pause--"></span> `pause()` (public)

called by the owner to pause, triggers stopped state



### <span id="Pausable-unpause--"></span> `unpause()` (public)

called by the owner to unpause, returns to normal state



### <span id="Pausable-Paused-address-"></span> `Paused(address account)`



### <span id="Pausable-Unpaused-address-"></span> `Unpaused(address account)`





## <span id="SafeMath"></span> `SafeMath`

Unsigned math operations with safety checks that revert on error

- [`mul(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-]
- [`div(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-]
- [`sub(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-]
- [`add(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-]
- [`mod(uint256 a, uint256 b)`][SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-]
### <span id="SafeMath-mul-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mul(uint256 a, uint256 b)  uint256` (internal)

Multiplies two unsigned integers, reverts on overflow.



### <span id="SafeMath-div-uint256-uint256-"></span> `div(uint256 a, uint256 b)  uint256` (internal)

Integer division of two unsigned integers truncating the quotient, reverts on division by zero.



### <span id="SafeMath-sub-uint256-uint256-"></span> `sub(uint256 a, uint256 b)  uint256` (internal)

Subtracts two unsigned integers, reverts on overflow (i.e. if subtrahend is greater than minuend).



### <span id="SafeMath-add-uint256-uint256-"></span> `add(uint256 a, uint256 b)  uint256` (internal)

Adds two unsigned integers, reverts on overflow.



### <span id="SafeMath-mod-uint256-uint256-"></span> `mod(uint256 a, uint256 b)  uint256` (internal)

Divides two unsigned integers and returns the remainder (unsigned integer modulo),  
reverts when dividing by zero.





## <span id="Ownable"></span> `Ownable`

The Ownable contract has an owner address, and provides basic authorization control  
functions, this simplifies the implementation of "user permissions".

- [`onlyOwner()`][Ownable-onlyOwner--]
- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(address sender)`][Ownable-initialize-address-]
- [`owner()`][Ownable-owner--]
- [`isOwner()`][Ownable-isOwner--]
- [`renounceOwnership()`][Ownable-renounceOwnership--]
- [`transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-transferOwnership-address-]
- [`_transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-]
- [`constructor()`][Context-constructor--]
- [`_msgSender()`][Context-_msgSender--]
- [`_msgData()`][Context-_msgData--]
- [`OwnershipTransferred(address previousOwner, address newOwner)`][Ownable-OwnershipTransferred-address-address-]
### <span id="Ownable-onlyOwner--"></span> `onlyOwner()`

Throws if called by any account other than the owner.

### <span id="Ownable-initialize-address-"></span> `initialize(address sender)` (public)

The Ownable constructor sets the original `owner` of the contract to the sender  
account.



### <span id="Ownable-owner--"></span> `owner()  address` (public)




#### *Returns*
- **the**: address of the owner.

### <span id="Ownable-isOwner--"></span> `isOwner()  bool` (public)




#### *Returns*
- **true**: if `msg.sender` is the owner of the contract.

### <span id="Ownable-renounceOwnership--"></span> `renounceOwnership()` (public)

Allows the current owner to relinquish control of the contract.  
It will not be possible to call the functions with the `onlyOwner`  
modifier anymore.  




### <span id="Ownable-transferOwnership-address-"></span> `transferOwnership(address newOwner)` (public)

Allows the current owner to transfer control of the contract to a newOwner.  


#### *Parameters*
- **newOwner**: The address to transfer ownership to.


### <span id="Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-"></span> `_transferOwnership(address newOwner)` (internal)

Transfers control of the contract to a newOwner.  


#### *Parameters*
- **newOwner**: The address to transfer ownership to.


### <span id="Ownable-OwnershipTransferred-address-address-"></span> `OwnershipTransferred(address previousOwner, address newOwner)`

## <span id="Initializable"></span> `Initializable`

Helper contract to support initializer functions. To use it, replace  
the constructor with a function that has the `initializer` modifier.  
WARNING: Unlike constructors, initializer functions must be manually  
invoked. This applies both to deploying an Initializable contract, as well  
as extending an Initializable contract via inheritance.  
WARNING: When used with inheritance, manual care must be taken to not invoke  
a parent initializer twice, or ensure that all initializers are idempotent,  
because this is not dealt with automatically as with constructors.

- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
### <span id="Initializable-initializer--"></span> `initializer()`

Modifier to use in the initializer function of a contract.



## <span id="Operator"></span> `Operator`

The Operator contract contains list of addresses authorized to specific administration operations on contracts  
  
Error messages  
OP01: Message sender must be an operator

- [`onlyOperator()`][Operator-onlyOperator--]
- [`onlyOwner()`][Ownable-onlyOwner--]
- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(address owner)`][Operator-initialize-address-]
- [`isOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-isOperator-address-]
- [`addOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-addOperator-address-]
- [`removeOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-removeOperator-address-]
- [`owner()`][Ownable-owner--]
- [`isOwner()`][Ownable-isOwner--]
- [`renounceOwnership()`][Ownable-renounceOwnership--]
- [`transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-transferOwnership-address-]
- [`_transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-]
- [`constructor()`][Context-constructor--]
- [`_msgSender()`][Context-_msgSender--]
- [`_msgData()`][Context-_msgData--]
- [`OperatorAdded(address operator)`][Operator-OperatorAdded-address-]
- [`OperatorRemoved(address operator)`][Operator-OperatorRemoved-address-]
- [`OwnershipTransferred(address previousOwner, address newOwner)`][Ownable-OwnershipTransferred-address-address-]
### <span id="Operator-onlyOperator--"></span> `onlyOperator()`

Throws OP01 if called by any account other than the operator

### <span id="Operator-initialize-address-"></span> `initialize(address owner)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **owner**: the final owner of the contract


### <span id="Operator-isOperator-address-"></span> `isOperator(address _operator)  bool` (public)

Checks if the address in param _operator is granted the operator right  


#### *Parameters*
- **_operator**: the address to check for operator right


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if the address is granted the operator right, false otherwise

### <span id="Operator-addOperator-address-"></span> `addOperator(address _operator)` (public)

Grants the operator right to _operator  


#### *Parameters*
- **_operator**: the address to grant


### <span id="Operator-removeOperator-address-"></span> `removeOperator(address _operator)` (public)

Removes the operator right from the _operator address  


#### *Parameters*
- **_operator**: the address of the operator to remove


### <span id="Operator-OperatorAdded-address-"></span> `OperatorAdded(address operator)`



### <span id="Operator-OperatorRemoved-address-"></span> `OperatorRemoved(address operator)`

## <span id="ComplianceRegistry"></span> `ComplianceRegistry`

The Compliance Registry stores user related attributes for multiple compliance authorities (named trusted intermediaries)  
  
Error messages  
UR01: UserId is invalid  
UR02: Address is already attached  
UR03: Users length does not match with addresses length  
UR04: Address is not attached  
UR05: Attribute keys length does not match with attribute values length  
UR06: Transfer and transfer decisions must have the same length  
UR07: Only originator can cancel transfer

- [`onlyOperator()`][Operator-onlyOperator--]
- [`onlyOwner()`][Ownable-onlyOwner--]
- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]

- [`isAddressValid(address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)`][ComplianceRegistry-isAddressValid-address---address-]
- [`isValid(address _trustedIntermediary, uint256 _userId)`][ComplianceRegistry-isValid-address-uint256-]

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-initialize-address-"></span> `initialize(address owner)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **owner**: the final owner of the contract


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-userId-address---address-"></span> `userId(address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256, address` (external)

fetch the userId associated to the provided address registered by trusted intermediaries  
The algorithm loops through each trusted intermediary and returns the first userId found   
even if the user exists for next trusted intermediaries  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trusted intermediaries to look the address for

- **_address**: address to look for


#### *Returns*
- **userId**: the user id found, 0 if not found

- **the**: address of the first trusted intermediary for which the user was found, 0x0 if no user was found

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-validUntil-address-uint256-"></span> `validUntil(address _trustedIntermediary, uint256 _userId)  uint256` (public)

returns the date at which user validity ends (UNIX timestamp)  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediary**: the reference trusted intermediary of the user

- **_userId**: the userId for which the validity date has to be returned


#### *Returns*
- **the**: date at which user validity ends (UNIX timestamp)

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-attribute-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `attribute(address _trustedIntermediary, uint256 _userId, uint256 _key)  uint256` (public)

get one user attribute  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediary**: the reference trusted intermediary of the user

- **_userId**: the userId for which the attribute has to be returned

- **_key**: the key of the attribute to return


#### *Returns*
- **the**: attribute value for the pair (_userId, _key), defaults to 0 if _key or _userId not found

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-attributes-address-uint256-uint256---"></span> `attributes(address _trustedIntermediary, uint256 _userId, uint256[] _keys)  uint256[]` (external)

access to multiple user attributes at once  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediary**: the reference trusted intermediary of the user

- **_userId**: the userId for which attributes have to be returned

- **_keys**: array of keys of attributes to return


#### *Returns*
- **the**: attribute values for each pair (_userId, _key), defaults to 0 if _key or _userId not found*

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-isAddressValid-address---address-"></span> `isAddressValid(address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  bool` (external)

Get the validaty of an address for trusted intermediaries  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trusted intermediaries to look the address for

- **_address**: address to look for


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if a user corresponding to the address was found for a trusted intermediary and is not expired, false otherwise

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-isValid-address-uint256-"></span> `isValid(address _trustedIntermediary, uint256 _userId)  bool` (public)

checks if the user id passed in parameter is not expired  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediary**: the reference trusted intermediary of the user

- **_userId**: the userId to be checked


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if a user was found for the trusted intermediary and is not expired, false otherwise

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-registerUser-address-uint256---uint256---"></span> `registerUser(address _address, uint256[] _attributeKeys, uint256[] _attributeValues)` (external)

Registers a new user corresponding to an address and sets its initial attributes  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Throws UR05 if _attributeKeys length is not the same as _attributeValues length  
Throws UR02 if address is already registered to a user  
Emits AddressAttached event  


#### *Parameters*
- **_address**: the address to register

- **_attributeKeys**: array of keys of attributes to set

- **_attributeValues**: array of values of attributes to set


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-registerUsers-address---uint256---uint256---"></span> `registerUsers(address[] _addresses, uint256[] _attributeKeys, uint256[] _attributeValues)` (external)

Registers multiple users corresponding to addresses and sets their initial attributes  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Ignores already registered addresses  
Throws UR05 if _attributeKeys length is not the same as _attributeValues length  
Emits multiple AddressAttached events  


#### *Parameters*
- **_addresses**: the array of addresses to register

- **_attributeKeys**: array of keys of attributes to set

- **_attributeValues**: array of values of attributes to set


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-attachAddress-uint256-address-"></span> `attachAddress(uint256 _userId, address _address)` (public)

Attach an address to an existing user  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Throws UR01 if user does not exist  
Throws UR02 if address is already attached  
Emits AddressAttached event  


#### *Parameters*
- **_userId**: the user id to which the address will be attached

- **_address**: the address to attach


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-attachAddresses-uint256---address---"></span> `attachAddresses(uint256[] _userIds, address[] _addresses)` (external)

Attach addresses to existing users  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Throws UR03 if _addresses length does not match _userIds length  
Throws UR02 if an address is already attached  
Throws UR01 if user does not exist  
Emits multiple AddressAttached events  


#### *Parameters*
- **_userIds**: array of user ids to which an address will be attached

- **_addresses**: array of addresses to attach


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-detachAddress-address-"></span> `detachAddress(address _address)` (public)

Detach an address from a user  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Throws UR04 if the address is not attached  
Emits AddressDetached event  


#### *Parameters*
- **_address**: address to detach


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-detachAddresses-address---"></span> `detachAddresses(address[] _addresses)` (external)

Detach addresses from their respective user  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Throws UR04 if an address is not attached  
Emits multiple AddressDetached events  


#### *Parameters*
- **_addresses**: array of addresses to detach


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-updateUserAttributes-uint256-uint256---uint256---"></span> `updateUserAttributes(uint256 _userId, uint256[] _attributeKeys, uint256[] _attributeValues)` (external)

Updates attributes for a user  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Throws UR05 if _attributeKeys length is not the same as _attributeValues length  
Throws UR01 user is not found  


#### *Parameters*
- **_userId**: the user id for which the attributes are updated

- **_attributeKeys**: array of keys of attributes to set

- **_attributeValues**: array of values of attributes to set


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-updateUsersAttributes-uint256---uint256---uint256---"></span> `updateUsersAttributes(uint256[] _userIds, uint256[] _attributeKeys, uint256[] _attributeValues)` (external)

Updates attributes for many users  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Throws UR05 if _attributeKeys length is not the same as _attributeValues length  
Ignores not found users  


#### *Parameters*
- **_userIds**: the user ids for which the attributes are updated

- **_attributeKeys**: array of keys of attributes to set

- **_attributeValues**: array of values of attributes to set


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-updateTransfers-address-address-address-uint256-"></span> `updateTransfers(address _realm, address _from, address _to, uint256 _value)  bool` (public)

Updates the transfer registry  
Intended to ba called by transfer computing rules that has been granted the operator right  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm (group) of the exchanged token

- **_from**: the sender of the tokens

- **_to**: the receiver of the tokens

- **_value**: transfered tokens value converted in CHF


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-monthlyTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `monthlyTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (external)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (IN and OUT) by an address for a 31 days period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (IN and OUT) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-yearlyTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `yearlyTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (external)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (IN and OUT) by an address for a 12 months period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (IN and OUT) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-monthlyInTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `monthlyInTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (external)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for a 31 days period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-yearlyInTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `yearlyInTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (external)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for a 12 months period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for the period for a specific realm

Returns the CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for a 31 days period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-yearlyOutTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `yearlyOutTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (external)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for a 12 months period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-addOnHoldTransfer-address-address-address-address-uint256-"></span> `addOnHoldTransfer(address trustedIntermediary, address token, address from, address to, uint256 amount)  bool` (public)

Adds a transfer to the on hold queue that will be processed by the trusted intermediary  
Intended to ba called by transfer computing rules that has been granted the operator right  
Emits a TransferOnHold event that can be listened by wallets for improved UX experience  


#### *Parameters*
- **trustedIntermediary**: the trusted intermediary for which the transfer is placed on hold

- **token**: the transfered token address

- **from**: the sender of the transfered tokens

- **to**: the receiver of the transfered tokens

- **amount**: the amount of transfered tokens


#### *Returns*
- **true**: is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-getOnHoldTransfers-address-"></span> `getOnHoldTransfers(address trustedIntermediary)  uint256 length, uint256[] id, address[] token, address[] from, address[] to, uint256[] amount` (public)

Fetch on hold transfers to be processed by a specific trusted intermediary  


#### *Parameters*
- **trustedIntermediary**: the trusted intermediary for which on hold transfers will be fetched


#### *Returns*
- **length**: the number of on hold transfers

- **id**: the array of ids for on hold transfers

- **token**: the array of token addresses for on hold transfers

- **from**: the array of sender addresses for on hold transfers

- **to**: the array of receiver addresses for on hold transfers

- **amount**: the array of amounts for on hold transfers

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-processOnHoldTransfers-uint256---uint8---"></span> `processOnHoldTransfers(uint256[] transfers, uint8[] transferDecisions)` (external)

Processes on hold transfers  
Intended to be called from a trusted intermediary key  
Transfer decision: 1 = Approve, 2 = Reject  
Emits either a TransferApproved or a TransferRejected event that can be listened by wallets for improved UX experience  
When transfer is approved, tokens are transfered to the receiver of the tokens  
When transfer is rejected, tokens are transfered back to the sender of the tokens  


#### *Parameters*
- **transfers**: array of transfer ids to process

- **transferDecisions**: array of transfer decisions applied to transfers


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-cancelOnHoldTransfers-address-uint256---"></span> `cancelOnHoldTransfers(address trustedIntermediary, uint256[] transfers)` (external)

Called by user to cancel transfers for a specific trusted intermediary and get his tokens back  
Throws UR07 if any of the transfer does not have user address as the sender  
Emits a TransferCancelled event that can be listened by wallets for improved UX experience  


#### *Parameters*
- **trustedIntermediary**: the trusted intermediary address for which the transfers are on hold

- **transfers**: array of transfer ids on hold with the trusted intermediary


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_approveOnHoldTransfer-uint256-"></span> `_approveOnHoldTransfer(uint256 transferIndex)` (internal)

Approves on hold transfer  


#### *Parameters*
- **transferIndex**: the id of the transfer to approve


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_rejectOnHoldTransfer-uint256-"></span> `_rejectOnHoldTransfer(uint256 transferIndex)` (internal)

Rejects on hold transfer  


#### *Parameters*
- **transferIndex**: the id of the transfer to reject


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_updateTransfers-address-address-address-uint256-"></span> `_updateTransfers(address _realm, address _from, address _to, uint256 _value)  bool` (internal)

Updates transfer history registries  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm (group) of the exchanged token

- **_from**: the sender of the tokens

- **_to**: the receiver of the tokens

- **_value**: transfered tokens value converted in CHF


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if sucessful, false otherwise

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_registerUser-address-uint256---uint256---"></span> `_registerUser(address _address, uint256[] _attributeKeys, uint256[] _attributeValues)` (internal)

Registers a new user corresponding to an address and sets its initial attributes  


#### *Parameters*
- **_address**: the address to register

- **_attributeKeys**: array of keys of attributes to set

- **_attributeValues**: array of values of attributes to set


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_updateUserAttributes-uint256-uint256---uint256---"></span> `_updateUserAttributes(uint256 _userId, uint256[] _attributeKeys, uint256[] _attributeValues)` (internal)

Updates attributes for a user  


#### *Parameters*
- **_userId**: the user id for which the attributes are updated

- **_attributeKeys**: array of keys of attributes to set

- **_attributeValues**: array of values of attributes to set


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_attachAddress-uint256-address-"></span> `_attachAddress(uint256 _userId, address _address)` (internal)

Attach an address to an existing user  


#### *Parameters*
- **_userId**: the user id to which the address will be attached

- **_address**: the address to attach


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_detachAddress-address-"></span> `_detachAddress(address _address)` (internal)

Detach an address from a user  


#### *Parameters*
- **_address**: address to detach


### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_isValid-address-uint256-"></span> `_isValid(address _trustedIntermediary, uint256 _userId)  bool` (internal)

Checks if the user id passed in parameter is not expired  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediary**: the reference trusted intermediary of the user

- **_userId**: the userId to be checked


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if a user was found for the trusted intermediary and is not expired, false otherwise

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_monthlyInTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `_monthlyInTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (internal)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for a 31 days period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for the period for a specific realm

Returns the CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for a 31 days period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_yearlyInTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `_yearlyInTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (internal)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for a 12 months period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup


#### *Returns*
- **the**: CHF amount transfered (IN) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_yearlyOutTransfers-address-address---address-"></span> `_yearlyOutTransfers(address _realm, address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256` (internal)

Returns the CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for a 12 months period for a specific realm  


#### *Parameters*
- **_realm**: the realm for which we want the amount to be returned

- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trustedIntermediaries in which we lookup the address

- **_address**: address to lookup

- **the**: CHF amount transfered (OUT) by an address for the period for a specific realm 

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_getUser-address---address-"></span> `_getUser(address[] _trustedIntermediaries, address _address)  uint256, address` (internal)

fetch the userId associated to the provided address registered by trusted intermediaries  
The algorithm loops through each trusted intermediary and returns the first userId found   
even if the user exists for next trusted intermediaries  


#### *Parameters*
- **_trustedIntermediaries**: array of trusted intermediaries to look the address for

- **_address**: address to look for


#### *Returns*
- **userId**: the user id found, 0 if not found

- **the**: address of the first trusted intermediary for which the user was found, 0x0 if no user was found

### <span id="ComplianceRegistry-_getMonth-uint256-"></span> `_getMonth(uint256 offset)  uint256` (internal)

Returns the month number based on the current date and the offset number of seconds in the past  
As we compute 31 days long month, it is assumed that the month number will not be accurate





## <span id="PriceOracle"></span> `PriceOracle`

The Price Oracle stores price related data for currency/token price conversion  
  
Error messages  
PO01: Pair length does not match price length   
PO02: Pair length does not match decimals length

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)

### <span id="PriceOracle-setPrices-bytes32---uint256---uint8---"></span> `setPrices(bytes32[] _pair, uint256[] _price, uint8[] _decimals)` (external)

Set prices for multiple pairs at the same time

- **_price**: array of prices

- **_decimals**: array of decimals of the price to be set


### <span id="PriceOracle-setPrice-bytes32-uint256-uint8-"></span> `setPrice(bytes32 _pair, uint256 _price, uint8 _decimals)` (public)

Set prices for multiple pairs at the same time  


#### *Parameters*
- **_pair**: pair of tokens/currencies to update the price for

- **_price**: new price

- **_decimals**: decimals of the price to be set


### <span id="PriceOracle-getPrice-bytes32-"></span> `getPrice(bytes32 _pair)  uint256, uint8` (public)

Get the price information for a specific pair of tokens/currencies  


#### *Parameters*
- **_pair**: pair of tokens/currencies to retrieve the price for


#### *Returns*
- **price**: price in decimals for the wanted pair

- **decimals**: number of decimals for the returns pair price

Get the price information for a specific pair of tokens/currencies  


#### *Parameters*

- **_currency2**: Second token/currency symbol string


#### *Returns*
- **price**: price in decimals for the wanted pair

- **decimals**: number of decimals for the returns pair price

#### *Returns*

Get the decimals for a specific pair of tokens/currencies  


#### *Parameters*
- **_pair**: pair of tokens/currencies to retrieve the decimals for


#### *Returns*
- **decimals**: last update date for the required pair

Get the bytes32 representation of a pair from two strings  


#### *Parameters*
- **_currency1**: First token/currency symbol string

- **_currency2**: Second token/currency symbol string


#### *Returns*
- **result**: the bytes32 representation of the concatenated strings



## <span id="Processor"></span> `Processor`

The Processor orchestrate most of the operations on each token  
  
Error messages  
TR01: Token already registered  
TR02: Empty name  
TR03: Empty symbol  
ER01: Cannot send tokens to 0x0  
ER02: Owner cannot be 0x0  
ER03: Spender cannot be 0x0  
RU03: Rule Engine rejected the transfer  
SE01: Cannot seize from 0x0  
SE02: Caller does not have the seizer role  
MT01: Cannot mint to 0x0  
MT03: Cannot redeem from 0x0  
SU01: Caller does not have the supplier role*

- [`onlyOperator()`][Operator-onlyOperator--]
- [`onlyOwner()`][Ownable-onlyOwner--]
- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(address owner, contract IRuleEngine _ruleEngine)`][Processor-initialize-address-contract-IRuleEngine-]
- [`setRuleEngine(contract IRuleEngine _ruleEngine)`][Processor-setRuleEngine-contract-IRuleEngine-]
- [`register(string _name, string _symbol, uint8 _decimals)`][Processor-register-string-string-uint8-]
- [`name()`][Processor-name--]
- [`symbol()`][Processor-symbol--]
- [`decimals()`][Processor-decimals--]
- [`totalSupply()`][Processor-totalSupply--]
- [`balanceOf(address _owner)`][Processor-balanceOf-address-]
- [`canTransfer(address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount)`][Processor-canTransfer-address-address-uint256-]
- [`transferFrom(address _from, address _to, uint256 _value)`][Processor-transferFrom-address-address-uint256-]
- [`approve(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _value)`][Processor-approve-address-address-uint256-]
- [`allowance(address _owner, address _spender)`][Processor-allowance-address-address-]
- [`increaseApproval(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _addedValue)`][Processor-increaseApproval-address-address-uint256-]
- [`decreaseApproval(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _subtractedValue)`][Processor-decreaseApproval-address-address-uint256-]
- [`seize(address _caller, address _account, uint256 _value)`][Processor-seize-address-address-uint256-]
- [`mint(address _caller, address _to, uint256 _amount)`][Processor-mint-address-address-uint256-]
- [`burn(address _caller, address _from, uint256 _amount)`][Processor-burn-address-address-uint256-]
- [`_addBalance(address _owner, uint256 _value)`][Processor-_addBalance-address-uint256-]
- [`_subBalance(address _owner, uint256 _value)`][Processor-_subBalance-address-uint256-]
- [`_setAllowance(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _value)`][Processor-_setAllowance-address-address-uint256-]
- [`initialize(address owner)`][Operator-initialize-address-]
- [`isOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-isOperator-address-]
- [`addOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-addOperator-address-]
- [`removeOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-removeOperator-address-]
- [`owner()`][Ownable-owner--]
- [`isOwner()`][Ownable-isOwner--]
- [`renounceOwnership()`][Ownable-renounceOwnership--]
- [`transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-transferOwnership-address-]
- [`_transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-]
- [`constructor()`][Context-constructor--]
- [`_msgSender()`][Context-_msgSender--]
- [`_msgData()`][Context-_msgData--]
- [`OperatorAdded(address operator)`][Operator-OperatorAdded-address-]
- [`OperatorRemoved(address operator)`][Operator-OperatorRemoved-address-]
- [`OwnershipTransferred(address previousOwner, address newOwner)`][Ownable-OwnershipTransferred-address-address-]
### <span id="Processor-initialize-address-contract-IRuleEngine-"></span> `initialize(address owner, contract IRuleEngine _ruleEngine)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **owner**: the final owner of the contract

- **_ruleEngine**: the rule engine library used by this processor


### <span id="Processor-setRuleEngine-contract-IRuleEngine-"></span> `setRuleEngine(contract IRuleEngine _ruleEngine)` (public)

Set the rule engine library used by this processor  


#### *Parameters*
- **_ruleEngine**: the rule engine library used by this processor


### <span id="Processor-register-string-string-uint8-"></span> `register(string _name, string _symbol, uint8 _decimals)` (external)

Registers a token with this processor  
Intended to be called by the token contract itself when initialized  
name, symbol and decimals are immutable  
Throws TR01 if the token is already registered with this processor  
Throws TR02 if the token name is empty  
Throws TR03 if the token symbol is empty  


#### *Parameters*
- **_name**: The token's name

- **_symbol**: The token's symbol

- **_decimals**: The token's number of decimals


### <span id="Processor-name--"></span> `name()  string` (public)

Returns the name of the token  
Intended to be called by the token contract  



#### *Returns*
- **name**: The name of the token

### <span id="Processor-symbol--"></span> `symbol()  string` (public)

Returns the symbol of the token  
Intended to be called by the token contract  



#### *Returns*
- **symbol**: The symbol of the token

### <span id="Processor-decimals--"></span> `decimals()  uint8` (public)

Returns the decimals of the token  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
For example, if `decimals` equals `2`, a balance of `505` tokens should  
be displayed to a user as `5,05` (`505 / 10 ** 2`).  



#### *Returns*
- **decimals**: The decimals of the token

### <span id="Processor-totalSupply--"></span> `totalSupply()  uint256` (public)

Returns the total supply of the token  
Intended to be called by the token contract  



#### *Returns*
- **totalSupply**: The total supply of the token

### <span id="Processor-balanceOf-address-"></span> `balanceOf(address _owner)  uint256` (public)

Returns the token balance for the address given in parameter  
Intended to be called by the token contract  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The address for which the balance has to be retrieved


#### *Returns*
- **balance**: The token balance for the address given in parameter

### <span id="Processor-canTransfer-address-address-uint256-"></span> `canTransfer(address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount)  bool, uint256, uint256` (public)

Determines whether a specific amount of tokens can be transfered from an address to another  
Intended to be called by the token contract  


#### *Parameters*
- **_from**: The sender of the tokens

- **_to**: The receiver of the tokens

- **_amount**: The amount of tokens to transfer


#### *Returns*
- **isValid**: True if the transfer is valid, false otherwise

- **ruleId**: The ruleId that first rejected the transfer

- **reason**: The reason code for the transfer rejection

### <span id="Processor-transferFrom-address-address-uint256-"></span> `transferFrom(address _from, address _to, uint256 _value)  bool, address updatedTo, uint256 updatedValue` (public)

Transfer a specific amount of tokens from an address to another  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
The receiver address and the amount can be updated by the token enforced rules  
Throws ER01 if receiver address is 0x0  
Throws RU03 if one of the rule rejects the transfer  


#### *Parameters*
- **_from**: The sender of the tokens

- **_to**: The intended receiver of the tokens

- **_value**: The intended amount of tokens to send


#### *Returns*
- **isSuccessful**: True if the transfer is successful, false otherwise

- **updatedTo**: The real address the tokens were sent to

- **updatedValue**: The real amount of tokens sent

### <span id="Processor-approve-address-address-uint256-"></span> `approve(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _value)  bool` (public)

Approves a specific amount of tokens to be spent by a spender from an address  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
Throws ER02 if owner address is 0x0  
Throws ER03 if spender address is 0x0  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The owner of the tokens to be allowed for spending

- **_spender**: The spender address to allow

- **_value**: The maximum amount of tokens that can be allowed for spending


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the approval is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="Processor-allowance-address-address-"></span> `allowance(address _owner, address _spender)  uint256` (public)

Returns the amount of tokens that are allowed to be spent by a spender from an address  
Intended to be called by the token contract  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The owner of the tokens to be spent

- **_spender**: The spender for which we want the allowed amount


#### *Returns*
- **The**: amount of tokens that can be spent by the spender from the owning address

### <span id="Processor-increaseApproval-address-address-uint256-"></span> `increaseApproval(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _addedValue)  bool` (public)

Increases the spending approval of tokens to be spent by a spender from an address by a specific amount  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
Throws ER02 if owner address is 0x0  
Throws ER03 if spender address is 0x0  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The owner of the tokens to be allowed for spending

- **_spender**: The spender address to allow

- **_addedValue**: The number of tokens for the approval increase


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the increase is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="Processor-decreaseApproval-address-address-uint256-"></span> `decreaseApproval(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _subtractedValue)  bool` (public)

Decreases the spending approval of tokens to be spent by a spender from an address by a specific amount  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
Throws ER02 if owner address is 0x0  
Throws ER03 if spender address is 0x0  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The owner of the tokens to be allowed for spending

- **_spender**: The spender address to allow

- **_subtractedValue**: The number of tokens for the approval decrease


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the decrease is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="Processor-seize-address-address-uint256-"></span> `seize(address _caller, address _account, uint256 _value)  bool` (public)

Seizes a specific amount of tokens from an address and transfers it to the caller address  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
Throws SE01 if the address for seize is 0x0  
Throws SE02 if the caller does not have the `Seizer` role  


#### *Parameters*
- **_caller**: The address that wants to seize the tokens

- **_account**: The address from which the tokens will be seized

- **_value**: The amount of tokens to seize


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the seize operation is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="Processor-mint-address-address-uint256-"></span> `mint(address _caller, address _to, uint256 _amount)  bool` (public)

Mints a specific amount of tokens to an address  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
Throws SU01 if the caller does not have the `Supplier` role  


#### *Parameters*
- **_caller**: The address that wants to mint tokens

- **_to**: The address on which the tokens will be minted

- **_amount**: The amount of tokens to mint


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the mint operation is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="Processor-burn-address-address-uint256-"></span> `burn(address _caller, address _from, uint256 _amount)  bool` (public)

Burns a specific amount of tokens to an address  
Intended to be called by the token contract  
Throws SU01 if the caller does not have the `Supplier` role  


#### *Parameters*
- **_caller**: The address that wants to burn tokens

- **_from**: The address from which the tokens will be burnt

- **_amount**: The amount of tokens to burn


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the burn operation is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="Processor-_addBalance-address-uint256-"></span> `_addBalance(address _owner, uint256 _value)` (internal)

Adds a specific amount of tokens to an address balance  
Intended to be called by the token contract  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The address on which the amount will be added

- **_value**: The amount fo tokens to add


### <span id="Processor-_subBalance-address-uint256-"></span> `_subBalance(address _owner, uint256 _value)` (internal)

Removes a specific amount of tokens to an address balance  
Intended to be called by the token contract  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The address from which the amount will be removed

- **_value**: The amount fo tokens to remove


### <span id="Processor-_setAllowance-address-address-uint256-"></span> `_setAllowance(address _owner, address _spender, uint256 _value)` (internal)

Sets the number of tokens that are allowed to be spent by the spender from the owner address  
Intended to be called by the token contract  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The owner of the tokens to be allowed for spending

- **_spender**: The spender address to allow

- **_value**: The maximum amount of tokens that can be allowed for spending




## <span id="RuleEngine"></span> `RuleEngine`

Rule Engine library defines rules that can be applied to all tokens restrict their transferability  
Errors:  
RE01: Rule id overflow*

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **owner**: the final owner of the contract


### <span id="RuleEngine-setRules-contract-IRule---"></span> `setRules(contract IRule[] rules)` (external)

set the rules of the library (replacing existing rules)  


#### *Parameters*
- **rules**: Array of rules that will replace the existing rules


### <span id="RuleEngine-ruleLength--"></span> `ruleLength()  uint256` (public)

Returns the number of rules in the library  



#### *Returns*
- **The**: number of rules in the library

### <span id="RuleEngine-rule-uint256-"></span> `rule(uint256 _ruleId)  contract IRule` (public)

Returns the rule associated to a specific id  
Throws RE01 if id is outside the rule array  


#### *Parameters*
- **_ruleId**: id of the rule to retrieve


#### *Returns*
- **rule**: Address of the rule

### <span id="RuleEngine-rules-uint256---"></span> `rules(uint256[] _ruleIds)  contract IRule[] result` (external)

Returns the rules associated to specific ids  
Throws RE01 if id is outside the rule array  


#### *Parameters*
- **_ruleIds**: Array of ids of the rules to retrieve


#### *Returns*
- **rules**: Array of addresses of the rules

### <span id="RuleEngine-validateTransferWithRules-uint256---uint256---address-address-address-uint256-"></span> `validateTransferWithRules(uint256[] _tokenRuleKeys, uint256[] _tokenRuleParams, address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount)  bool isValid, uint256 ruleId, uint256 reason` (external)

Check if a transfer is valid according to the rules and rule parameters passed in parameters  


#### *Parameters*
- **_tokenRuleKeys**: Array of rule ids that have to be checked

- **_tokenRuleParams**: Array of rule parameters that are enforced for rules

- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_amount**: Amount of token to transfer


#### *Returns*
- **isValid**: True if the transfer is valid according to all rules, false otherwise

- **ruleId**: Id of the first invalid rule

- **reason**: Code representing the rule rejection reason

## <span id="HardTransferLimitRule"></span> `HardTransferLimitRule`

HardTransferLimitRule checks the different transfer thresholds of the  
attached compliance registry for the from and to addresses and rejects the  
transfer if any of the thresholds are broken  
  
Thresholds:  
- Transfer threshold  
- Monthly transfer threshold (30 days moving period)  
- Yearly transfer threshold (12 * 30 days moving period)  
  
Error messages  
RU02: Function cannot be called  
  
Errors  
1: from address not found in User Registry  
2: from user single transfer limit exceeded  
3: from user monthly transfer limit exceeded  
4: from user yearly transfer limit exceeded  
5: to address not found in User Registry  
6: to user single transfer limit exceeded  
7: to user monthly transfer limit exceeded  
8: to user yearly transfer limit exceeded

- [`onlyOperator()`][Operator-onlyOperator--]
- [`onlyOwner()`][Ownable-onlyOwner--]
- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(address owner, contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)`][HardTransferLimitRule-initialize-address-contract-IComplianceRegistry-]
- [`isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256 _noCheckThreshold)`][HardTransferLimitRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][HardTransferLimitRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`afterTransferHook(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256)`][HardTransferLimitRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`_isTransferValid(address _token, address realm, address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256 _noCheckThresholdDecimals)`][HardTransferLimitRule-_isTransferValid-address-address-address---address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`_isTransferFromValid(address realm, address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _address, uint256 _amountInRefCurrency, uint256 _noCheckThresholdDecimals)`][HardTransferLimitRule-_isTransferFromValid-address-address---address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`_isTransferToValid(address realm, address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _address, uint256 _amountInRefCurrency, uint256 _noCheckThresholdDecimals)`][HardTransferLimitRule-_isTransferToValid-address-address---address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`initialize(address owner)`][Operator-initialize-address-]
- [`isOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-isOperator-address-]
- [`addOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-addOperator-address-]
- [`removeOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-removeOperator-address-]
- [`owner()`][Ownable-owner--]
- [`isOwner()`][Ownable-isOwner--]
- [`renounceOwnership()`][Ownable-renounceOwnership--]
- [`transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-transferOwnership-address-]
- [`_transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-]
- [`constructor()`][Context-constructor--]
- [`_msgSender()`][Context-_msgSender--]
- [`_msgData()`][Context-_msgData--]
- [`OperatorAdded(address operator)`][Operator-OperatorAdded-address-]
- [`OperatorRemoved(address operator)`][Operator-OperatorRemoved-address-]
- [`OwnershipTransferred(address previousOwner, address newOwner)`][Ownable-OwnershipTransferred-address-address-]
### <span id="HardTransferLimitRule-initialize-address-contract-IComplianceRegistry-"></span> `initialize(address owner, contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **owner**: the final owner of the contract

- **_complianceRegistry**: The Compliance Registry address that will be used by this rule for compliance checks 


### <span id="HardTransferLimitRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256 _noCheckThreshold)  uint256, uint256` (public)

Validates a transfer if transfer amounts (single, monthly, yearly) are below the thresholds  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_amount**: Amount of tokens to send

- **_noCheckThreshold**: Threshold above which we apply this rule


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Invalid transfer when thresholds are broken, valid transfer with after hook action when transfer is allowed

- **statusCode**: The reason of the transfer rejection indicating which threshold is broken

### <span id="HardTransferLimitRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)  uint256, address, uint256` (external)

Dummy before transfer hook  
Not intended to be called  
Throws RU02 because this function is not intended to be called



### <span id="HardTransferLimitRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `afterTransferHook(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256)  bool` (external)

Updates the compliance registry transfer counters after the transfer happened  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_amount**: Amount of tokens to send


### <span id="HardTransferLimitRule-_isTransferValid-address-address-address---address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `_isTransferValid(address _token, address realm, address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256 _noCheckThresholdDecimals)  uint256 isValid, uint256 reason` (internal)

Checks if the transfer is valid

## <span id="SoftTransferLimitRule"></span> `SoftTransferLimitRule`

SoftTransferLimitRule checks the different transfer thresholds of the  
attached compliance registry for the from and to addresses and reroute the  
transfer to the Compliance Registry where the transfer will be on-hold for  
for processing by one of the trusted authorities  
  
Thresholds:  
- Transfer threshold  
- Monthly transfer threshold (30 days moving period)  
- Yearly transfer threshold (12 * 30 days moving period)  
  
Error messages  
RU02: Function cannot be called  
SR01: from address not found in User Registry  
  
Errors  
1: from address not found in User Registry  
2: from user single transfer limit exceeded  
3: from user monthly transfer limit exceeded  
4: from user yearly transfer limit exceeded  
5: to address not found in User Registry  
6: to user single transfer limit exceeded  
7: to user monthly transfer limit exceeded  
8: to user yearly transfer limit exceeded

- [`onlyOperator()`][Operator-onlyOperator--]
- [`onlyOwner()`][Ownable-onlyOwner--]
- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(address owner, contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)`][SoftTransferLimitRule-initialize-address-contract-IComplianceRegistry-]
- [`isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256 _noCheckThreshold)`][SoftTransferLimitRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`beforeTransferHook(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256)`][SoftTransferLimitRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`afterTransferHook(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256)`][SoftTransferLimitRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`_isTransferValid(address _token, address realm, address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256 _noCheckThresholdDecimals)`][SoftTransferLimitRule-_isTransferValid-address-address-address---address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`_isTransferFromValid(address realm, address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _address, uint256 _amountInRefCurrency, uint256 _noCheckThresholdDecimals)`][SoftTransferLimitRule-_isTransferFromValid-address-address---address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`_isTransferToValid(address realm, address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _address, uint256 _amountInRefCurrency, uint256 _noCheckThresholdDecimals)`][SoftTransferLimitRule-_isTransferToValid-address-address---address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`initialize(address owner)`][Operator-initialize-address-]
- [`isOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-isOperator-address-]
- [`addOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-addOperator-address-]
- [`removeOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-removeOperator-address-]
- [`owner()`][Ownable-owner--]
- [`isOwner()`][Ownable-isOwner--]
- [`renounceOwnership()`][Ownable-renounceOwnership--]
- [`transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-transferOwnership-address-]
- [`_transferOwnership(address newOwner)`][Ownable-_transferOwnership-address-]
- [`constructor()`][Context-constructor--]
- [`_msgSender()`][Context-_msgSender--]
- [`_msgData()`][Context-_msgData--]

### <span id="SoftTransferLimitRule-initialize-address-contract-IComplianceRegistry-"></span> `initialize(address owner, contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **owner**: the final owner of the contract

- **_complianceRegistry**: The Compliance Registry address that will be used by this rule for compliance checks 


### <span id="SoftTransferLimitRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256 _noCheckThreshold)  uint256, uint256` (public)

Validates a transfer if transfer amounts (single, monthly, yearly) are below the thresholds  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_amount**: Amount of tokens to send

- **_noCheckThreshold**: Threshold above which we apply this rule


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Valid transfer with before hook action when thresholds are broken, valid transfer with after hook action when transfer is allowed

- **statusCode**: The reason of the transfer rejection indicating which threshold is broken

### <span id="SoftTransferLimitRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `beforeTransferHook(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256)  uint256, address, uint256` (external)

Reroutes the transfer to the Compliance Registry where the transfer will be on-hold for  
for processing by one of the trusted authorities  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_amount**: Amount of tokens to send


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Valid transfer with before hook action

- **updatedTo**: Address of the compliance registry where the tokens will be held 
before processing by one of the trusted authorities

- **updatedAmount**: Initial transfer amount. The amount is not changed by this rule

### <span id="SoftTransferLimitRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `afterTransferHook(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256 _amount, uint256)  bool` (external)

Updates the compliance registry transfer counters after the transfer happened  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_amount**: Amount of tokens to send

Checks if the transfer is valid for the receiver address





## <span id="UserFreezeRule"></span> `UserFreezeRule`

FreezeRule allows trusted authorities to enforce a freeze of assets for specific addresses  
  
Error messages  
RU02: Function cannot be called  
  
Errors  
2: from address is frozen for send operations  
3: to address is frozen for receive operations

- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)`][UserFreezeRule-initialize-contract-IComplianceRegistry-]
- [`isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256, uint256)`][UserFreezeRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][UserFreezeRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`afterTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][UserFreezeRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`_canSend(address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _from)`][UserFreezeRule-_canSend-address---address-]
- [`_canReceive(address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _to)`][UserFreezeRule-_canReceive-address---address-]
### <span id="UserFreezeRule-initialize-contract-IComplianceRegistry-"></span> `initialize(contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **_complianceRegistry**: The Compliance Registry address that will be used by this rule for compliance checks


### <span id="UserFreezeRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256, uint256)  uint256, uint256` (public)

Validates a transfer if the from address can send the tokens (not frozen for send) and the to address can receive it (not frozen for receive)  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Invalid transfer if one of the address is frozen, valid transfer without further action otherwise

- **statusCode**: The reason of the transfer rejection indicating which address is frozen

### <span id="UserFreezeRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)  uint256, address, uint256` (external)

Dummy before transfer hook  
Not intended to be called  
Throws RU02 because this function is not intended to be called



### <span id="UserFreezeRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `afterTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)  bool` (external)

Dummy after transfer hook  
Not intended to be called  
Throws RU02 because this function is not intended to be called



### <span id="UserFreezeRule-_canSend-address---address-"></span> `_canSend(address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _from)  bool` (internal)

Checks if an address can send tokens  


#### *Parameters*
- **trustedIntermediaries**: array of trusted intermediaries defined at the token level

- **_from**: address to check


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the address can send, false otherwise

### <span id="UserFreezeRule-_canReceive-address---address-"></span> `_canReceive(address[] trustedIntermediaries, address _to)  bool` (internal)

Checks if an address can receive tokens  


#### *Parameters*
- **trustedIntermediaries**: array of trusted intermediaries defined at the token level

- **_to**: address to check


#### *Returns*
- **True**: if the address can receive, false otherwise



## <span id="UserKycThresholdBothRule"></span> `UserKycThresholdBothRule`

UserKycThresholdBothRule checks if receiver and sender KYC of a transfer are above a specific KYC threshold   
and rejects the transfer if not  
  
Error messages  
RU02: Function cannot be called  
  
Errors  
1: from address not found in User Registry  
2: from Kyc level is less than threshold  
3: to address not found in User Registry  
4: to Kyc level is less than threshold

- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)`][UserKycThresholdBothRule-initialize-contract-IComplianceRegistry-]
- [`isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256, uint256 _kycThreshold)`][UserKycThresholdBothRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][UserKycThresholdBothRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`afterTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][UserKycThresholdBothRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
### <span id="UserKycThresholdBothRule-initialize-contract-IComplianceRegistry-"></span> `initialize(contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **_complianceRegistry**: The Compliance Registry address that will be used by this rule for compliance checks


### <span id="UserKycThresholdBothRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256, uint256 _kycThreshold)  uint256, uint256` (public)

Validates a transfer if the from and to addresses KYC levels are above the defined threshold  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_kycThreshold**: The KYC level threshold defined at the token rule level


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Invalid transfer if KYC levels are below the threshold, valid transfer without further action otherwise

- **statusCode**: The reason of the transfer rejection

## <span id="UserValidRule"></span> `UserValidRule`

UserValidRule checks if sender/receiver addresses of a transfer  
are known and valid in the compliance registry and rejects the transfer if not  
  
Error messages  
RU02: Function cannot be called  
  
Errors:  
1: unsupported flag  
2: invalid from address  
3: invalid to address

- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize(contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)`][UserValidRule-initialize-contract-IComplianceRegistry-]
- [`isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256, uint256 _userValidFlag)`][UserValidRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][UserValidRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`afterTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][UserValidRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
### <span id="UserValidRule-initialize-contract-IComplianceRegistry-"></span> `initialize(contract IComplianceRegistry _complianceRegistry)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **_complianceRegistry**: The Compliance Registry address that will be used by this rule for compliance checks


### <span id="UserValidRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `isTransferValid(address _token, address _from, address _to, uint256, uint256 _userValidFlag)  uint256, uint256` (public)

Validates a transfer if from/to addresses are known and valid  


#### *Parameters*
- **_token**: Address of the contract that represent the token to be transfered

- **_from**: Sender address

- **_to**: Receiver address

- **_userValidFlag**: Flag indicating which address to check (0 = Both, 1 = From, 2 = To)


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Invalid transfer if one of the addresses is not known or not valid, valid transfer without further action otherwise

- **statusCode**: The reason of the transfer rejection

### <span id="UserValidRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)  uint256, address, uint256` (external)

Not intended to be called  
Throws RU02 because this function is not intended to be called





## <span id="YesNoRule"></span> `YesNoRule`

YesNoRule validates transfer if param _yesNo is more than 0

Errors:  
1: _yesNo param is 0

Validates a transfer is the _yesNo parameters is more than 0  


#### *Parameters*
- **_yesNo**: parameter that determines the validity of the transfer


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Invalid transfer _yesNo is 0, valid transfer without further action otherwise

## <span id="YesNoUpdateRule"></span> `YesNoUpdateRule`

YesNoUpdateRule validates transfer if param _yesNo is more than 0  
The rule always answer the same response through isValid  
Calling the updateAfterTransfer function will increment updateCount  
Useful for testing implementation  
  
Error messages  
RU02: Function cannot be called  
  
Errors:  
1: _yesNo param is 0

- [`initializer()`][Initializable-initializer--]
- [`initialize()`][YesNoUpdateRule-initialize--]
- [`isTransferValid(address, address, address, uint256, uint256 _yesNo)`][YesNoUpdateRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][YesNoUpdateRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`afterTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)`][YesNoUpdateRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-]
### <span id="YesNoUpdateRule-initialize--"></span> `initialize()` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  
Set the update count to 0



### <span id="YesNoUpdateRule-isTransferValid-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `isTransferValid(address, address, address, uint256, uint256 _yesNo)  uint256, uint256` (public)

Validates a transfer is the _yesNo parameters is more than 0  


#### *Parameters*
- **_yesNo**: parameter that determines the validity of the transfer


#### *Returns*
- **transferStatus**: Invalid transfer _yesNo is 0, valid transfer with after hook action otherwise

- **statusCode**: The reason of the transfer rejection

### <span id="YesNoUpdateRule-beforeTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `beforeTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)  uint256, address, uint256` (external)

Dummy before transfer hook  
Not intended to be called  
Throws RU02 because this function is not intended to be called



### <span id="YesNoUpdateRule-afterTransferHook-address-address-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `afterTransferHook(address, address, address, uint256, uint256)  bool` (external)

### <span id="BridgeERC20-transfer-address-uint256-"></span> `transfer(address _to, uint256 _value)  bool` (public)

transfer token for a specified address  


#### *Parameters*

- **_value**: The amount to be transferred.


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if transfer is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="BridgeERC20-balanceOf-address-"></span> `balanceOf(address _owner)  uint256` (public)

Gets the balance of the specified address.  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: The address to query the the balance of.


#### *Returns*
- **An**: uint256 representing the amount owned by the passed address.

### <span id="BridgeERC20-transferFrom-address-address-uint256-"></span> `transferFrom(address _from, address _to, uint256 _value)  bool` (public)

Transfer tokens from one address to another  


#### *Parameters*
- **_from**: address The address which you want to send tokens from

- **_to**: address The address which you want to transfer to

- **_value**: uint256 the amount of tokens to be transferred


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if transfer is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="BridgeERC20-approve-address-uint256-"></span> `approve(address _spender, uint256 _value)  bool` (public)

Approve the passed address to spend the specified amount of tokens on behalf of msg.sender.  
  
Beware that changing an allowance with this method brings the risk that someone may use both the old  
and the new allowance by unfortunate transaction ordering. One possible solution to mitigate this  
race condition is to first reduce the spender's allowance to 0 and set the desired value afterwards:  
https://github.com/ethereum/EIPs/issues/20#issuecomment-263524729  


#### *Parameters*
- **_spender**: The address which will spend the funds.

- **_value**: The amount of tokens to be spent.


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if approval is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="BridgeERC20-allowance-address-address-"></span> `allowance(address _owner, address _spender)  uint256` (public)

Function to check the amount of tokens that an owner allowed to a spender.  


#### *Parameters*
- **_owner**: address The address which owns the funds.

- **_spender**: address The address which will spend the funds.


#### *Returns*
- **A**: uint256 specifying the amount of tokens still available for the spender.

### <span id="BridgeERC20-increaseApproval-address-uint256-"></span> `increaseApproval(address _spender, uint256 _addedValue)  bool` (public)

Increase the amount of tokens that an owner allowed to a spender.  
  
approve should be called when allowed[_spender] == 0. To increment  
allowed value is better to use this function to avoid 2 calls (and wait until  
the first transaction is mined)  
From MonolithDAO Token.sol  


#### *Parameters*
- **_spender**: The address which will spend the funds.

- **_addedValue**: The amount of tokens to increase the allowance by.


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if increase is successful, false otherwise

### <span id="BridgeERC20-decreaseApproval-address-uint256-"></span> `decreaseApproval(address _spender, uint256 _subtractedValue)  bool` (public)

Decrease the amount of tokens that an owner allowed to a spender.  
  
approve should be called when allowed[_spender] == 0. To decrement  
allowed value is better to use this function to avoid 2 calls (and wait until  
the first transaction is mined)  
From MonolithDAO Token.sol  


#### *Parameters*
- **_spender**: The address which will spend the funds.

- **_subtractedValue**: The amount of tokens to decrease the allowance by.


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if decrease is successful, false otherwise

## <span id="VotingSession"></span> `VotingSession`

VotingSession enables the organisation of a voting session  
  
Error messages  
VO01: names length is not the same as urls length  
VO02: names length is not the same as proposals length  
VO03: voters length is not the same as weights length  
VO04: delegate cannot be 0x0  
VO05: caller not allowed has delegate  
VO06: voter has not been invited to vote  
VO07: Resolution id overflow  
VO08: Proposal id overflow  
VO09: Proposal already voted  
VO10: Voting session is not open  
VO11: Voting session has already been open

- [`whenVotingSessionOpen()`][VotingSession-whenVotingSessionOpen--]
- [`beforeVotingSession()`][VotingSession-beforeVotingSession--]
- [`onlyOperator()`][Operator-onlyOperator--]

- [`resolutionCount()`][VotingSession-resolutionCount--]
- [`registerVoters(address[] _voters, uint256[] _weights)`][VotingSession-registerVoters-address---uint256---]
- [`setVotingPeriod(uint256 _start, uint256 _end)`][VotingSession-setVotingPeriod-uint256-uint256-]
- [`delegateVote(address delegate)`][VotingSession-delegateVote-address-]
- [`vote(address voter, uint256 resolutionId, uint256 proposalId)`][VotingSession-vote-address-uint256-uint256-]
- [`getResolutionResults(uint256 resolutionId)`][VotingSession-getResolutionResults-uint256-]
- [`hasVotedForResolution(address voter, uint256 resolutionId)`][VotingSession-hasVotedForResolution-address-uint256-]
- [`isOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-isOperator-address-]
- [`addOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-addOperator-address-]
- [`removeOperator(address _operator)`][Operator-removeOperator-address-]
