### <span id="VotingSession-whenVotingSessionOpen--"></span> `whenVotingSessionOpen()`

Throws VO10 if called when voting is not open yet

### <span id="VotingSession-beforeVotingSession--"></span> `beforeVotingSession()`

Throws VO11 if called after voting session starts

### <span id="VotingSession-initialize-address-"></span> `initialize(address owner)` (public)

Initializer (replaces constructor when contract is upgradable)  


#### *Parameters*
- **owner**: the final owner of the contract


### <span id="VotingSession-addResolutions-bytes32---bytes32---uint256---"></span> `addResolutions(bytes32[] _names, bytes32[] _urls, uint256[] _proposalCounts)` (external)

Adds a new set of resolutions to the voting session  
Throws VO01 if names length is not the same as urls length  
Throws VO02 if names length is not the same as proposal counts length  
Throws VO11 if the voting session has already started  


#### *Parameters*
- **_names**: Array of vote names

- **_urls**: Array of bytes where each vote details can be found

- **_proposalCounts**: Array containing the count of proposals for each vote (proposals should be detailed in the vote url)


### <span id="VotingSession-resolutionCount--"></span> `resolutionCount()  uint256` (public)

Returns the number of resolutions in the voting session  



#### *Returns*
- **resolutionCount**: Number of resolutions in the voting session

### <span id="VotingSession-registerVoters-address---uint256---"></span> `registerVoters(address[] _voters, uint256[] _weights)` (external)

Set the addresses allowed to vote with their respective weight  
Throws VO02 if voters length is not the same as weights length  
Throws VO11 if the voting session has already started  


#### *Parameters*
- **_voters**: array of addresses allowed to vote

- **_weights**: array of weigths, each weight corresponding to a voter


### <span id="VotingSession-setVotingPeriod-uint256-uint256-"></span> `setVotingPeriod(uint256 _start, uint256 _end)` (public)

Set the voting period  
Throws VO11 if the voting session has already started  


#### *Parameters*
- **_start**: Start timestamp of the voting period

- **_end**: End timestamp of the voting period


### <span id="VotingSession-delegateVote-address-"></span> `delegateVote(address delegate)` (public)

Allows a voter or potential voter to delegate their vote to another address  
Throws VO03 if the delegate is 0x0  
Throws VO11 if the voting session has already started  


#### *Parameters*
- **delegate**: The address of the delegate


### <span id="VotingSession-vote-address-uint256-uint256-"></span> `vote(address voter, uint256 resolutionId, uint256 proposalId)` (public)

Allows a voter (or his delegate) to vote for a proposal in a vote  
Throws VO05 if function caller is not allowed to vote for voter (not voter or not delegate)  
Throws VO06 if voter has not been registered  
Throws VO07 if resolution id overflows  
Throws VO08 if proposal id overflows  
Throws VO09 if voter has already voted for this resolution  


#### *Parameters*
- **voter**: the final voter address 

- **resolutionId**: Id of the resolution to vote for

- **proposalId**: Id of the proposal to vote for


### <span id="VotingSession-getResolutionResults-uint256-"></span> `getResolutionResults(uint256 resolutionId)  uint256[]` (public)

Returns the proposals results for a vote  
Throws VO07 if resolution id overflows  


#### *Parameters*
- **resolutionId**: Id of the resolution


#### *Returns*
- **array**: of result for each proposal

### <span id="VotingSession-hasVotedForResolution-address-uint256-"></span> `hasVotedForResolution(address voter, uint256 resolutionId)  bool` (public)

Returns if a voter has voted for a specific resolution  
Throws VO07 if resolution id overflows  


#### *Parameters*
- **voter**: Address of the voter

- **resolutionId**: Id of the resolution


#### *Returns*
- **true**: if the voter has voted, false otherwise

### <span id="VotingSession-ResolutionAdded-bytes32-bytes32-uint256-"></span> `ResolutionAdded(bytes32 name, bytes32 url, uint256 proposalCount)`



### <span id="VotingSession-VoterRegistered-address-uint256-"></span> `VoterRegistered(address voter, uint256 weight)`



### <span id="VotingSession-VotingPeriodSet-uint256-uint256-"></span> `VotingPeriodSet(uint256 votingStart, uint256 votingEnd)`



### <span id="VotingSession-Vote-address-uint256-uint256-uint256-"></span> `Vote(address voter, uint256 resolutionId, uint256 proposalId, uint256 weight)`
